[08.09.23, 15:14:38] Jesper: bool unload(void)
{
    // DONE
    for (int i = 0; i < N; i++)
    {
        node *next_node = table[i];

        while (next_node != NULL)
        {
            node* tmp_node = next_node;
            next_node = next_node->next;
            free(tmp_node);
        }
    }
    return true;
}
